<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Who We Are &#8211; US Travel Experts</h2>



<p style="font-size:18px">We’re Eva and JP, an age-gap couple road-tripping our way across the U.S., one weekend getaway at a time.</p>



<p>Since 2020, we’ve been sharing our best travel tips, hidden gem destinations, and budget-friendly hacks, all backed by 20+ years of combined experience in the travel industry, from theme parks and hotels to guided vacations and tourism planning.</p>



<p>Our mission? To make travel easy, affordable, and accessible, no matter your budget or schedule. We specialize in <a href="https://discoveringhiddengems.com/road-trips/" data-type="link" data-id="https://discoveringhiddengems.com/road-trips/" data-wpel-link="internal"><strong>U.S. road trips</strong></a> and weekend escapes, helping you travel smarter.</p>



<p style="font-size:18px">🎉 Ready to hit the road? Grab our FREE <strong><a href="https://discovering-hidden-gems.kit.com/insiderseries" data-type="link" data-id="https://discovering-hidden-gems.kit.com/insiderseries" rel="noopener follow external noreferrer" data-wpel-link="external" target="_blank">Discount Travel Secrets Insider Series</a></strong> and start traveling more for less today!</p>
